                Date.prototype.to_iso_with_offset = function() {
                    var time_zone_offset = -this.getTimezoneOffset(),
                        time_zone_diff = time_zone_offset >= 0 ? '+' : '-',
                        pad = function(num) {
                            var norm = Math.floor(Math.abs(num));
                            return (norm < 10 ? '0' : '') + norm;
                        };
                    return this.getFullYear() +
                        '-' + pad(this.getMonth() + 1) +
                        '-' + pad(this.getDate()) +
                        'T' + pad(this.getHours()) +
                        ':' + pad(this.getMinutes()) +
                        ':' + pad(this.getSeconds()) +
                        time_zone_diff + pad(time_zone_offset / 60) +
                        ':' + pad(time_zone_offset % 60);

				    <script>
                        require(["knockout", "jquery", "models/showcase-player", "underscore", "vanillaLazyLoad", "sidearm-responsive"], function (ko, $, ShowcasePlayer, _, LazyLoad) {
                            $(window).sidearmResponsive();

                            var vm = function() {
                                var self = this;

                                self.templates = ko.observableArray([
                                    {id: 1, label: "Roster View - List"},
                                    {id: 2, label: "Roster View - Grid"},
                                    {id: 3, label: "Roster View - Cards"},
                                ]);

                                self.default_template = _.find(self.templates(), function(template){
                                    return template.id == 3;
                                });

                                self.active_template = ko.observable(self.default_template);
                                self.active_template_temp = ko.observable(self.default_template);

                                self.active_template.subscribe(function(){
                                    setTimeout(function(){
                                        $.sidearm.sidearmResponsive();
                                        imglazyload.update();
                                        $(window).trigger('scroll');
                                    },0);
                                });
                                
                                self.switch_template = function () {
                                    self.active_template(self.active_template_temp());
                                };

                                self.togglePlayer = function (data, event) {
                                    var $element = $(event.currentTarget),
                                        player_id = $element.data('player-id'),
                                        player_url = $element.data('player-url'),
                                        player_hide_bio = ((typeof $element.data('player-hide-bio')) !== 'undefined');

                                    if ($element.find('.sidearm-roster-player-extra').length == 0) {
                                        var _player = new Player(player_id, player_url, player_hide_bio);
                                        var $extra = $('#sidearm-roster-player-extra-original').clone().removeAttr('id');
                                        $element.append($extra);
                                        ko.applyBindings(_player, $extra[0]);
                                    }

                                    $element.toggleClass("show-extra").find('.sidearm-roster-player-extra').slideToggle(250);                 
                                };
                            };

                            $(document).on("keydown", ".sidearm-roster-player-toggle", function(e) {

                                var $this = $(this),
                                    $parent = $this.parent(),
                                    key = e.which,
                                    shift = e.shiftKey;

                                if (key === 13 || key === 32) {

                                    setTimeout(function(){

                                        if ($parent.hasClass("show-extra")) {
                                            $parent.find('.sidearm-roster-player-extra a:visible, .sidearm-roster-player-extra button:visible').first().focus();
                                        }

                                    }, 350);

                                }

                            }).on("focusin", "a, button, select, input, option", function (e) {

                                var $this = $(this);

                                        e.preventDefault();

                                if ( $(".sidearm-roster-default-template .sidearm-roster-player.show-extra").length && $this.closest(".sidearm-roster-player-extra").length <= 0 ) {

                                    $(".sidearm-roster-default-template .sidearm-roster-player.show-extra .sidearm-roster-player-extra").hide();
                                    $(".sidearm-roster-default-template .sidearm-roster-player.show-extra").removeClass("show-extra");

                                }

                            });

                            

				            var sharedVm = new vm();

                            var Player = function (id, url, hide_bio) {
			                    var self = this;

			                    self.isLoading = ko.observable(true);
                                self.id = id;
                                self.hideBio = hide_bio;
			                    self.stats = ko.observableArray();
			                    self.stories = ko.observableArray();
                                self.pressclips = ko.observableArray();
                                self.url = url;
			                    $.getJSON('/services/responsive-roster.ashx', { player_id: id, sport_id: '2', sport_shortname: 'softball', year: '2022' }, function (response) {
			                        if (response === null || response.stats === null)
			                            self.stats(null);
			                        else {
			                            response.stats.map(function (stat) {
			                                self.stats.push(new Stat(stat));
			                            });
			                            self.stats()[0].selected(true);
			                        }

			                        if (response === null || response.stories === null || response.stories.length === 0)
			                            self.stories(null);
			                        else {
			                            var stories = ko.utils.arrayMap(response.stories, function (story) {
			                                self.stories.push(new Story(story));
			                            });
			                        }

			                        self.isLoading(false);
			                    });

			                    self.selectStatCategory = function (stat) {
			                        for (var i = 0; i < self.stats().length; i++)
			                            self.stats()[i].selected(false);
			                        stat.selected(true);
			                    };
			                };

			                var Stat = function (data) {
			                    var self = this;

			                    self.title = data.title;
			                    self.title_short = data.title_short;
			                    self.headings = data.headings;
			                    self.data = data.data;

			                    self.selected = ko.observable(false);                
			                }

			                var Story = function (data) {
			                    var self = this;

			                    self.id = data.id,
						        self.headline = data.headline,
						        self.teaser = data.teaser,
						        self.date = data.date,
						        self.image = data.image,
						        self.image_alt_text = data.image_alt_text,
						        self.url = data.url,
						        self.video = data.video
										        ? new ShowcasePlayer({ youtube: data.youtube, Archive: data.Archive })
										        : null;
			                }

                            var PressClips = function (data) {
			                    var self = this;

			                    self.id = data.id,
						        self.title = data.title,
						        self.author = data.author,
						        self.summary = data.summary,
                                self.date = data.date,
                                self.date = data.datedisplay,
						        self.image = data.image,
						        self.image_alt_text = data.image_alt_text,
						        self.url = data.url
			                }

			                ko.applyBindings(sharedVm, $('.sidearm-roster-templates-container')[0]);
			                ko.applyBindings(sharedVm, $('.sidearm-roster-header')[0]);

                            $(function() {

                                $(document).on('click', '#sidearm-list-sort-by-button', function(e) {
                                    e.preventDefault();
                                    var url = $('#ddl_past_rosters').val() + "?&sort=" + $('#ctl00_cplhMainContent_ddl_sort_options').val();
                                    window.location = url ;
                                });
                                
                                //download dropdown keyboard focus
                                $(document).on("focusin focusout", ".sidearm-roster-view .sidearm-roster-header-download ul a", function (e) {
                                    if (e.type === "focusin") {
                                        $(this).closest(".sidearm-roster-header-download").addClass("sidearm-hover");
                                    } else if (e.type === "focusout") {
                                        $(this).closest(".sidearm-roster-header-download").removeClass("sidearm-hover");
                                    }
                                });

                            });
						  
                            $('.sidearm-roster-select-year .sidearm-select-button').on("click", function(e) {
                                e.preventDefault();
                                var url = $('.sidearm-roster-select-year select').val();
                                window.location = url;
                            });

                            var imglazyload = new LazyLoad({
                                elements_selector: ".lazy",
                                data_src: "original"
                            });

                        });
                    </script>

<script>
    require(['jquery'], function($) {
        var scrollTimer = null;
    
        function hide_ads() {
            $('html').addClass('sticky-leaderboard-is-hidden');
        };
        
        function scrolled() {
            scrollTimer = null;
            if($(window).scrollTop() > 300){
                $('html').addClass('sticky-leaderboard-is-hidden');
            } else {
                $('html').removeClass('sticky-leaderboard-is-hidden');
            }
        };
    
        setTimeout(
            function(){
                $(window).scroll(function(){
                    if (scrollTimer) {
                        clearTimeout(scrollTimer);
                    }
                    scrollTimer = setTimeout(scrolled, 500);
                })
        }, 5000);
    });
</script>

        transform: translate(0, 100%);
    }
    
    .c-sticky-leaderboard .dfp-ad {
        margin: 0 auto;
    }

                        $('html').headroom('destroy').removeData('headroom').headroom({ "offset": 96 });
                    }
                    else if (window.matchMedia('(min-width: 0px)').matches){
                        $('html').headroom('destroy').removeData('headroom').headroom({ "offset": 0 });
                    }
                }).trigger('resize');

                $(document).on("keyup", ".c-scoreboard__toggle", function(e) {
                    var key = e.which;
                    //Tab
                    if (key === 9) {
                        
                        //$('.c-scoreboard__list')[0].slick();

                    }
                });


                /**
                *
                *
                */
                $.fn.SidearmAccessibleSlickSliders = function () {


                    //Prepend this string to all console.log output
                    var preConsoleLog = "SidearmAccessibleSlickSliders >>> ";


                    //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "Initializing");


                    var selectors = [
                        "content-stream-component",
                        "stories-component",
                        "twitter-component",
                        "instagram-component",
                        "galleries-component",
                        "facebook-component",
                        "ads-component",
                        "events-component",
                        "results-component",
                        "scoreboard-component",
                        "fanatics-component",
                        "youtube-component",
                        "slideshow-component",
                        "all-access-component",
                        "#pressclippings-section",
                        "#topStories"
                    ];


                    $(selectors.join(", ")).each(function (index, element) {


                        var $selected = $(this);
                        
                        if ($selected.closest(".sidearm-accessibility-do-not-process").length <= 0) {


                            $selected.keyup(function (e) {


                                var key = e.which,
                                    $selected_keyup = $(this),
                                    index = 0,
                                    $slick = $selected_keyup.find(".slick-slider"),
                                    $focus = $(':focus'),
                                    active = false,
                                    nofocus = false;


                                if (key === 9) {
                                    
                                    if ($slick.length) {


                                        if (!$slick.hasClass("sidearm-accessible-slick")) {


                                            $slick.slick("slickGoTo", (0), false);
                                            
                                            if ($selected_keyup.closest(".slick-slide").length) {
                                                $slick.find("[data-slick-index='" + 0 + "']").find("a").first().focus();
                                                active = true;
                                            }
                                            
                                            if ($selected_keyup.closest(".slick-slider").length >= 1) {
                                                active = true;
                                            }


                                            if ($focus.closest(".slick-slide").length) {
                                                active = true;
                                            }
                                            
                                            //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "active", active);
                                            
                                            SidearmAccessibleSlick($slick, active);


                                            $slick.on("keydown", ".slick-slide a, .slick-slide button", function (e) {


                                                var key = e.which,
                                                    $this = $(this),
                                                    index = 0,
                                                    $slick = $this.closest(".slick-slider"),
                                                    $slickSlide =  $this.closest(".slick-slide"),
                                                    thisIndex = $.trim($slickSlide.attr("data-slick-index")),
                                                    slickLength = $(".slick-slide:not('.slick-cloned')", $slick).length;


                                                //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "slickLength = " + slickLength);


                                                if (key === 9) {


                                                    //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "Tab");


                                                    if ($slick.length) {


                                                        if (!$slick.hasClass("sidearm-accessible-slick")) {


                                                            $slick.slick("slickGoTo", (0), false);


                                                            if ($(':focus').closest(".slick-slide").length) {


                                                                index = parseInt($(':focus').closest(".slick-slide").data("slick-index"));


                                                                if (index < 0) {
                                                                    $slick.find("[data-slick-index='" + 0 + "']").find("a").not(".sidearm-tabindex-negative").first().focus();
                                                                }


                                                            }


                                                            SidearmAccessibleSlick($slick, false);


                                                        } else {


                                                            //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "already paused");


                                                            var $links = $("a:not([tabindex='-1']), button:not([tabindex='-1'])", $slickSlide),
                                                                linkIndex = $links.index($this),
                                                                linkIndexGoTo = 0,
                                                                slickIndex = 0;
                                                                
                                                            //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "linkIndex: " + linkIndex);


                                                            if (e.shiftKey) {
                                                                
                                                                linkIndex = linkIndex - 1;
                                                                
                                                                if (linkIndex >= 0) {
                                                                    
                                                                    if (typeof $links[linkIndex] !== "undefined") {
                                                                        if ($links[linkIndex].closest(".slick-slide").length > 0) {
                                                                            
                                                                            slickIndex = parseInt($links[linkIndex].closest(".slick-slide").attr("data-slick-index"));
                                                                            linkIndexGoTo = linkIndex - 1;
                                                                            
                                                                            if (linkIndexGoTo === 0) {
                                                                                if (slickIndex >= 0 && slickIndex < slickLength) {
                                                                                    e.preventDefault();
                                                                                    //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "End of links, go to previous slide.");
                                                                                    $slick.slick("slickGoTo", (slickIndex), false);
                                                                                    setTimeout(function () {
                                                                                        $slick.find("[data-slick-index='" + slickIndex + "']").find("a:not([tabindex='-1']), button:not([tabindex='-1'])").not(".sidearm-tabindex-negative").last().focus();
                                                                                    }, 10);
                                                                                }
                                                                            }
                                                                            
                                                                        }
                                                                    }
                                                                    
                                                                } else {
                                                                    
                                                                    slickIndex = parseInt($this.closest(".slick-slide").attr("data-slick-index"));
                                                                    
                                                                    if ((slickIndex - 1) >= 0 /*&& (slickIndex != parseInt(thisIndex))*/) {
                                                                        
                                                                        var $prevLink = $slick.find("[data-slick-index='" + (slickIndex - 1) + "']").find("a:not([tabindex='-1']), button:not([tabindex='-1'])").not(".sidearm-tabindex-negative").last();
                                                                        
                                                                        if ($prevLink.length) {
                                                                        
                                                                            e.preventDefault();
                                                                            //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "slide has 1 link, go to previous slide.");
                                                                            $slick.slick("slickGoTo", (slickIndex - 1), false);
                                                                            setTimeout(function () {
                                                                                $prevLink.focus();
                                                                            }, 10);
                                                                        
                                                                        } else {
                                                                            
                                                                            $prevLink = $slick.find("[data-slick-index='" + (slickIndex - 2) + "']").find("a:not([tabindex='-1']), button:not([tabindex='-1'])").not(".sidearm-tabindex-negative").last();
                                                                            
                                                                            if ($prevLink.length) {
                                                                            
                                                                                e.preventDefault();
                                                                                //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "slide has 1 link, go to previous slide (skipping no link slide).");
                                                                                $slick.slick("slickGoTo", (slickIndex - 2), false);
                                                                                setTimeout(function () {
                                                                                    $prevLink.focus();
                                                                                }, 10);
                                                                            
                                                                            }
                                                                            
                                                                        }
                                                                    
                                                                    }
                                                                    
                                                                }
                                                                
                                                            } else {
                                                                
                                                                linkIndex = linkIndex + 1;


                                                                if (typeof $links[linkIndex] !== "undefined") {
                                                                    
                                                                    if ($links[linkIndex].closest(".slick-slide").length > 0) {
                                                                        slickIndex = $links[linkIndex].closest(".slick-slide").attr("data-slick-index");
                                                                        linkIndexGoTo = linkIndex + 1;
                                                                        if (linkIndexGoTo === ($links.length)) {
                                                                            if (slickIndex >= 0 && slickIndex < slickLength) {
                                                                                e.preventDefault();
                                                                                //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "End of links, go to next slide.");
                                                                                $slick.slick("slickGoTo", (slickIndex), false);
                                                                                setTimeout(function () {
                                                                                    $slick.find("[data-slick-index='" + slickIndex + "']").find("a:not([tabindex='-1']), button:not([tabindex='-1'])").not(".sidearm-tabindex-negative").first().focus();
                                                                                }, 10);
                                                                            }
                                                                        }
                                                                    }
                                                                    
                                                                } else {
                                                                    
                                                                    slickIndex = parseInt($this.closest(".slick-slide").attr("data-slick-index"));
                                                                    
                                                                    if ((slickIndex + 1) < slickLength) {
                                                                        
                                                                        var $nextFocus = $slick.find("[data-slick-index='" + (slickIndex + 1) + "']").find("a:not([tabindex='-1']):visible, button:not([tabindex='-1']):visible").not(".sidearm-tabindex-negative").first();
                                                                        
                                                                        if ($nextFocus.length) {
                                                                            e.preventDefault();
                                                                            //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "slide has 1 link, go to next slide. $nextFocus: ", $nextFocus);
                                                                            $slick.slick("slickGoTo", (slickIndex + 1), false);
                                                                            setTimeout(function () {
                                                                                $nextFocus.focus();
                                                                            }, 10);
                                                                        }
                                                                        
                                                                    }
                                                                    


                                                                }


                                                            }


                                                        }


                                                    }


                                                }


                                            });


                                        }
                                    }
                                }


                            });
                        
                        }


                    });


                    if (typeof window.SidearmAccessibleSlickSlidersOptions === "undefined") {
                        window.SidearmAccessibleSlickSlidersOptions = {
                            timer: 0,
                            timerInterval: 100,
                            timerStop: 3000,
                            navTestOne: false,
                            navTestTwo: false,
                            navTestThree: false
                        };
                    }


                    if (typeof window.SidearmAccessibleSlickSlidersLoop === "undefined") {
                        window.SidearmAccessibleSlickSlidersLoop = setInterval(loop, window.SidearmAccessibleSlickSlidersOptions.timerInterval);
                    }


                    function loop() {


                        var options = window.SidearmAccessibleSlickSlidersOptions;


                        $("stories-component").find(".prev-arrow").attr("aria-label", "Previous Slide");
                        $("stories-component").find(".next-arrow").attr("aria-label", "Next Slide");


                        //Increment timer counter
                        options.timer = options.timer + options.timerInterval;


                        //Exit out of loop if time is up
                        if (options.timer >= options.timerStop) {
                            //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "Loop finished.");
                            clearInterval(window.SidearmAccessibleSlickSlidersLoop);
                        }


                    }


                };//$.fn.SidearmAccessibleSlickSliders






                /**
                *
                * @param {any} $slick
                */
                function SidearmAccessibleSlick ($slick, active) {


                    //Prepend this string to all console.log output
                    var preConsoleLog = "SidearmAccessibleSlick >>> ";


                    //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "Initializing: ", $slick);


                    if ($slick.length) {


                        if (!$slick.hasClass("sidearm-accessible-slick")) {


                            try {


                                $("[tabindex='0']", $slick).removeAttr("tabindex");


                                //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "pausing animation");


                                $slick.addClass("sidearm-accessible-slick");


                                $slick.slick("slickPause");


                                $slick.slick("slickSetOption", "speed", "1");


                                $slick.on('afterChange', function (event, slick, currentSlide) {
                                    //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "currentSlide: ", currentSlide);
                                    //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "$(slick.$slides[currentSlide]): ", $(slick.$slides[currentSlide]));
                                });


                                //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "Disabling buttons");
                                
                                $(".slick-prev", $slick).on("keydown", function (e) {
                                    
                                    var $prev = $(this),
                                        key = e.which,
                                        shift = e.shiftKey;
                                        
                                    if (key == 9 && shift) {
                                        
                                        var $active = $slick.find(".slick-slide.slick-active").last();
                                        
                                        if ($active.find("a") <= 0) {
                                        
                                            e.preventDefault();
                                            
                                            if ($active.length) {
                                                
                                                if ($active.is("a") || $active.is("button")) {
                                                    
                                                    $active.focus();
                                                    
                                                } else {
                                                    
                                                    if ($active.find("a").length) {
                                                        
                                                        $active.find("a").first().focus();
                                                    
                                                    } else if ($active.find("button").length) {
                                                    
                                                        $active.find("button").first().focus();
                                                    
                                                    }
                                                    
                                                }
                                                
                                            }
                                            
                                        }
                                        
                                    }
                                    
                                });


                                $(".slick-cloned a, .slick-cloned button, a.slick-cloned", $slick).attr("tabindex", "-1");


                                $(".slick-cloned", $slick).html("");


                                if (active) {
                                    
                                    var index = parseInt( $(".slick-slide:not(.slick-cloned) a", $slick).first().closest(".slick-slide").attr("data-slick-index") );


                                    if (index >= 0) {


                                        //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "Going to first link in slide " + index);


                                        $slick.slick("slickGoTo", index, true);
                                        $slick.find("[data-slick-index='" + index + "'] a:not([tabindex='-1']), [data-slick-index='" + index + "'] button:not([tabindex='-1'])").first().focus();


                                    } else {
                                        
                                        index = parseInt( $("a.slick-slide:not(.slick-cloned)", $slick).first().attr("data-slick-index") );
                                        
                                        if (index >= 0) {
                                            
                                            $slick.slick("slickGoTo", index, true);
                                            $slick.find("a[data-slick-index='" + index + "']").first().focus();
                                            
                                        }
                                        
                                    }
                                    
                                } else {
                                    
                                    //testing this commented out (2020-03-05)
                                    ////window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog + "finding first focusable element");
                                    //$("a:not([tabindex='-1']), button:not([tabindex='-1'])", $slick).first().focus();
                                    
                                }


                            }
                            catch (err) {


                                // Do nothing
                                //window.SidearmConsoleLog(SidearmLineNumber(), preConsoleLog, err);


                            }


                        }


                    }


                }//SidearmAccessibleSlick()




                $(window).SidearmAccessibleSlickSliders();


                /**
                * Detect Keyboard Navigation
                */
                window.SidearmFirstTabPress = true;
                $(document).on("keyup keydown keypress", "body, nav, nav a, nav button, a", function (e) {
                    
                    var $this = $(this),
                        key = e.which,
                        $search = $(".gsc-results-wrapper-visible").not(".gsc-results-wrapper-nooverlay");
                    
                    if (key === 9 && $this.not("input") && $this.not("textarea") && !$("body").hasClass("sidearm-keyboard-navigation")) {
                        
                        $("body").addClass("sidearm-keyboard-navigation");
                        
                        if ($search.length && window.SidearmFirstTabPress) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            $search.find("a").first().focus();
                        }
                        
                        window.SidearmFirstTabPress = false;
                        
                    }
                    
                });


                function is_keyboard () {
                    return $("body").hasClass("sidearm-keyboard-navigation");
                }


                function is_mobile () {
                    
                    if ( $(".main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation-desktop .c-navigation__url--level-1").length ) {

                        return false;

                    } else {
                        
                        return true;

                    }

                }


                $(document).on("focusin", ".main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation-mobile a", function (e) {

                    var $this = $(this),
                        $li = $this.closest("li"),
                        $container = $(".main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation-mobile .c-navigation__offcanvas");
                        $containerStar = $(".main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation-mobile .c-navigation__offcanvas > *");

                    //console.log('focusin', $li.offset().top, $this);

                    setTimeout(function() {

                        // Position of first element relative to container top
                        var scrollTop = $this.offset().top - $container.offset().top;

                        // Position of selected element relative to container top
                        var targetTop = $containerStar.offset().top - $container.offset().top;

                        // The offset of a scrollable container
                        var scrollOffset = scrollTop - targetTop;

                        // Scroll untill target element is at the top of its container
                        $container.scrollTop(scrollOffset);

                        //$container.animate({ scrollTop: (scrollOffset) }, 250);

                        //$('.main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation-mobile .c-navigation__offcanvas').animate({ scrollTop: ($this.offset().top) }, 200);
                        //$('.main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation-mobile .c-navigation__offcanvas').scrollTop($this.offset().top);

                    }, 1);

                }).on("focusin", ".s-stories .c-stories--slider .c-stories__media .showcase-play-button", function (e) {

                    //.s-stories .c-stories--slider .c-stories__media .showcase-play-button


                });


                


                var infiniteLoop = setInterval(function(){
        
                    $(".slick-list[tabindex]").removeAttr("tabindex");

                    $(".slick-cloned a:not([tabindex='-1'])").attr("tabindex", "-1").attr("aria-hidden", "true");
                    $("a.slick-cloned:not([tabindex='-1'])").attr("tabindex", "-1").attr("aria-hidden", "true");

                    $(".slick-cloned button:not([tabindex='-1'])").attr("tabindex", "-1").attr("aria-hidden", "true");
                    $("button.slick-cloned:not([tabindex='-1'])").attr("tabindex", "-1").attr("aria-hidden", "true");

                    $(".slick-cloned:not([aria-hidden='true'])").attr("aria-hidden", "true");
                    $(".slick-slide[aria-hidden]:not(.slick-cloned)").removeAttr("aria-hidden");

                    //$("#s-events__tabs .s-events__tabs-container > li:not([tabindex='0'])").attr("tabindex", "0");

                    
                    $(".slick-pause-play:not(.a11y-moved)").each(function( index ) {
                                        
                        var $pause = $(this),
                            $prev = $pause.parent().find(".slick-prev");

                        $pause.insertAfter($prev);
                        $pause.addClass("a11y-moved");

                    });

                    $(".s-sponsors .ads-container .ad.slick-cloned:not(.a11y-hide-cloned)").css({
                        'height': 0,
                        'overflow': 'hidden'
                    }).addClass("a11y-hide-cloned");

                    //$(".dfp-ad iframe:not(.a11y-tabindex)").attr("tabindex", "-1").attr("aria-hidden", "true").addClass("a11y-tabindex");
                    

                    $(".s-main-tabs .c-tabs--main .ui-tabs-panel[aria-hidden='true'] a, .s-main-tabs .c-tabs--main .ui-tabs-panel[aria-hidden='true'] button").attr("tabindex", "-1");
                    $(".s-main-tabs .c-tabs--main .ui-tabs-panel[aria-hidden='false'] a, .s-main-tabs .c-tabs--main .ui-tabs-panel[aria-hidden='false'] button").attr("tabindex", "0");

                }, 250);


                $(document).on("focusin", "a, button, input, select, option, iframe, [tabindex]", function (e) {

                    var $this = $(this);

                    if ( $(".s-scoreboard .c-scoreboard--slider .c-scoreboard__overlay.is-open").length && $this.closest(".c-scoreboard__overlay").length <= 0 ) {

                        $(".s-scoreboard .c-scoreboard--slider .c-scoreboard__toggle.is-toggled").click();

                    }

                }).on("focusin", ".s-scoreboard .c-scoreboard--slider .c-scoreboard__toggle, .s-stories .c-stories__item a, .s-stories .c-stories__item button, .s-promo-rotator .ads-container .ad a, .s-slideshow .c-slideshow--promo .c-slideshow__link, .s-sponsors .ads-container .ad a", function (e) {

                    /*var $this = $(this),
                        $slick = $this.closest(".slick-slider"),
                        $slide = $this.closest(".slick-slide"),
                        index = $.trim($slide.attr("data-slick-index"));


                    if (index >= 0) {
                        console.log("slickGoTo", index);
                        $slick.slick("slickPause");
                        $slick.slick("slickGoTo", parseInt(index), false);
                        $slick.slick("slickPause");
                    }*/

                }).on("click", ".main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation__toggle", function (e) {

                    var $this = $(this),
                        open = $this.hasClass("is-toggled");

                    if (open && is_keyboard()) {

                        e.preventDefault();
                        $(".main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation-mobile .c-navigation__url--level-1").first().focus();

                    }

                }).on("keydown", ".main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation-mobile .c-navigation__url--level-1:first", function (e) {

                    var $this = $(this),
                        key = e.which,
                        shift = e.shiftKey;

                    if (key == 9 && shift) {

                        e.preventDefault();
                        $(".main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation__toggle").first().focus();

                    }

                }).on("keydown", ".main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation-mobile .c-navigation__url--level-1:last, .main-navigation .c-navigation--main .c-navigation-mobile .c-navigation__url--level-2:last", function (e) {

                    var $this = $(this),
                        key = e.which,
                        shift = e.shiftKey;

                    if (key == 9 && !shift) {

                        if ($(".c-search--overlay .c-search__toggle").length) {

                            e.preventDefault();
                            $(".c-search--overlay .c-search__toggle").first().focus();

                        }

                    }



                });

                function SidearmAccessibleVideoPopUpWait() {
                
                    if ($.fn.SidearmAccessibleVideoPopUp) {
                
                        $(document).SidearmAccessibleVideoPopUp({
                            buttonPlay: ".s-videos .c-videos--grid .c-videos__play-btn",
                            buttonClose: ".s-videos .c-videos--grid .showcase-modal__close",
                            iframe: ".s-videos .c-videos--grid .showcase-modal .showcase-video-player"
                        });
                
                    } else {
                
                        setTimeout(function() { SidearmAccessibleVideoPopUpWait() }, 5);
                
                    }
                
                }//SidearmAccessibleVideoPopUpWait()
                
                SidearmAccessibleVideoPopUpWait();




                


            });

    <script type='text/html' id='template-promotions'><!-- ko ifnot: isInitializing() -->

    <!-- ko switch -->

        <!-- ko case: ad.location.type === 'single' -->
            <!-- ko with: single -->
                <div class="ad single-ad" data-bind="css: css_class">
                    <!-- ko if: link === '' || link === '#' -->
                        <span>
                            <picture data-bind="html5Picture: picture, alt: ((typeof picture.images[0] != 'undefined') ? (picture.images[0].alt) : (hover_text ? hover_text : title))"></picture>
                        </span>
                    <!-- /ko -->
                    <!-- ko if: link !== '' && link !== '#' -->
                        <a data-bind="
                            attr:{
                                'aria-label': ((typeof picture.images[0] != 'undefined') ? (picture.images[0].alt) : (hover_text ? hover_text : title)), 
                                href: link, 
                                title: hover_text ? hover_text : title, 
                                target: open_in_new_window ? '_blank' : '', 
                                click: $component.trackEvent.bind($data, 'click', $data.title),
                                'tabindex' : ko.computed(function() {
                                    var index = 
                                    $parents.findIndex(function(item) {
                                        return Object.keys(item).length > 0 && item.component;
                                    });
                                    if(index < 0)
                                        return 0;

                                    var model = $parents[index];
                                    if(model.component.name != 'main-nav')
                                        return 0;
                                    if (model.component.name === 'main-nav')
                                        return model.isMenuOpen() ? '0' : '-1';
                                    return 0;
                                })
                            },
                            event: {
                                focus: function() {
                                    var index = 
                                    $parents.findIndex(function(item) {
                                        return Object.keys(item).length > 0 && item.component;
                                    });
                                    if(index < 0)
                                        return;

                                    var model = $parents[index];
                                    if (model.component.name === 'main-nav') {
                                        model.openMenu();
                                    }
                                    return;
                                },
                                blur: function() {
                                    var index = 
                                    $parents.findIndex(function(item) {
                                        return Object.keys(item).length > 0 && item.component;
                                    });
                                    if(index < 0)
                                        return;

                                    var model = $parents[index];
                                    if (model.component.name === 'main-nav') {
                                        model.closeMenu();
                                    }
                                    return;
                                }
                            }
                            ">
                            <picture data-bind="html5Picture: picture, alt: ((typeof picture.images[0] != 'undefined') ? (picture.images[0].alt) : (hover_text ? hover_text : title))"></picture>
                            <!-- ko if: open_in_new_window -->
                                <span class="external-link a11y-hide">Opens in new window</span>
                            <!-- /ko -->
                        </a>
                    <!-- /ko -->
                </div>
            <!-- /ko -->

                    <script>
                        window.preloaded_templates_are_rendering = true;

                        require(['knockout'], function (ko) {
                            function register_custom_loader(component, vm_name, template_name) {
                                if (document.getElementById('template-' + (template_name || component) )) {
                                    var custom_loader = {
                                        getConfig: function(name, callback) {
                                            if (name === component + '-component') {
                                                componentConfig = {
                                                    template: { element: 'template-' + (template_name || component) },
                                                    viewModel: { require: 'components/' + (vm_name || component) }
                                                };
                                                callback(componentConfig);
                                            }
                                            else {
                                                callback(null)
                                            }
                                        }
                                    };

                                    ko.components.loaders.unshift(custom_loader);
                                }
                            }

                            register_custom_loader('ads', 'promotions', 'promotions');
                            register_custom_loader('dfp', 'evergreen', 'evergreen');

                            register_custom_loader('scoreboard');
register_custom_loader('navigation');
register_custom_loader('search');

                            
                            window.preloaded_templates_are_rendering = false;
                        });
                    </script>

<script>
    var host_element = document.querySelector(".b5acvg143-modal__text-host");
    host_element.href = window.location.href; 
    host_element.innerText = window.location.hostname; 

    function close_banner() {
        var CookieDate = new Date;
        CookieDate.setTime(CookieDate.getTime() + 1 * 3600 * 1000 * 24);
        document.cookie = "sidearm-adblock-banner_consent=true; expires=\"" + CookieDate.toGMTString() + "\";";
        document.querySelector(".b5acvg143").remove();
    }

    var consent_button = document.querySelector(".b5acvg143-banner__consent");

    consent_button.addEventListener("click", function() { close_banner(); });

    require(['config'], function(config) {
        require(['jquery', 'knockout', 'cookie', 'text'], function ($, ko, cookie, text) {
            $(function () {   
                //disable check for Siteimprove scans
                if (navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf('siteimprove') < 0) {
                    
                    if (cookie.get_cookie('sidearm-adblock-banner_consent')) {
                        return;
                    }

                    var deferred = $.Deferred();
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "HEAD",
                        async: true,
                        url: "/components/js/analytics.js",
                    }).done(function(message,text,jqXHR){
                        deferred.resolve();
                    })
                    .fail(function(err){
                        show_ad_blocker_blocked_modal();
                        deferred.reject();
                    });

                    deferred.then(function(success) {
                        $.get('/common/templates/dfp/dfp-component-template.html')
                            .then(function (response) {
                            }, function (error) {
                                show_ad_blocker_blocked_modal();
                            });
                    }, function (error) {
                        show_ad_blocker_blocked_modal()
                    })
                    .fail(function(){
                        show_ad_blocker_blocked_modal()
                    });

                    function show_ad_blocker_blocked_modal() {
                        var modal = document.querySelector('.b5acvg143');
                        modal.style.display = 'flex';
                        modal.querySelector('.b5acvg143-banner__consent').focus();
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    });
</script>
